border-box;\">而在穆里尼奥则是另一种状态。</span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(56, 53, 53);box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(56, 53, 53);box-sizing: border-box;\">早年的穆里尼奥，也曾是“齐天大圣”，意气风发、目中无人。</span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(56, 53, 53);box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(56, 53, 53);box-sizing: border-box;\">与弗格森斗、与温格斗、与巴萨斗、与形形色色“内鬼”斗，语录从“特殊的一个”一路发展到“球队遗产论”，总有一副狂到没边的意气。</span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(56, 53, 53);box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(56, 53, 53);box-sizing: border-box;\">但即便是那个“狂人”，也没有如孔蒂般与高层为敌，没有在很多层面固执地一塌糊涂。</span></section><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section></section><section 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">全国拥有150家门店的威尔仕健身是国内中高端健身品牌之一，该品牌旗下的国际化一站式时尚健身会所Wfitness by Will's、高端奢华健身馆VIP by Will's等，吸引了全国超过130多万会员。</span></section><section 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">威尔仕健身品牌经理王敏君分析说：“这次疫情加速了行业的变革，是危机，更是机会。危机的点是消费需求在缩减，大家不敢去，也少去公共场所了，中小型健身房面临倒闭的风险；与此同时居家健身在崛起，行业在洗牌。”</span></section><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1.2282609\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"828\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">7月底，在徐汇区的亚洲旗舰店徐汇苑新开张。王敏君说：“我们原本计划今年开50家门店，年底规模达到200家，但因为疫情影响，我们会减少开店的数量，同时对现有门店进行服务提升和升级，稳扎稳打。”</span></section><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;margin: 20px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;align-self: stretch;flex: 10 10 0%;background-color: rgb(255, 248, 246);height: auto;padding-top: 5px;padding-bottom: 5px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: center;font-size: 21px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.6;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">03</strong></p></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 80px;border-style: solid;border-width: 3px;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgb(255, 137, 89);flex: 0 0 auto;align-self: stretch;height: auto;margin-top: -15px;margin-right: -77px;margin-bottom: -15px;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;background-color: rgb(255, 248, 246);flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: stretch;border-width: 0px;height: auto;padding: 5px 10px;border-top-style: solid;border-top-left-radius: 0px;border-top-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">个人品牌的培养转型</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1.8px;padding-right: 10px;padding-left: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">由于门店的关闭，一批健身从业者失去了工作，不得不重新找寻落脚点甚至改行。</span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">但是一些有客户的从业人员也面临新的机会。</span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">上世纪90年代，张军伟在北京开启了职业健身教练之路。</span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">他是国内最早接受系统美国健身理念的教练之一。2008年，张军伟飞赴亚特兰大参加CrossFit教练培训，成为首个通过这一培训的中国人。现在在业内，人们都叫他做Jet。</span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">受疫情影响， Jet供职了近20年的健身房关闭了，但他每天却依旧很忙。因为他的会员们，依旧习惯跟他一起训练。</span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">唯一的变化是，训练地点变成了线上或在开放的公园里。</span></section><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">“健身应该是寻求健康的体魄、提升生活品质，实际上是一种生活的刚需，而不是单纯的减脂塑形。”Jet说道。</span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">“会员里有好几个都跟了我10多年了，我不能辜负了他们，所以我们正在筹建自己的工作室，这将是未来的一个趋势，小而精，这样的工作室更能彰显教练的专业度而非销售能力。”</span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">八年前，康东旭从健美爱好者转型成为了健身从业者，参加非诚勿扰提升了他的知名度。此后，他和多个综艺节目合作，并为在《乘风破浪的姐姐》里秀了一把火辣身材的钟丽缇担任教练。</span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">在疫情期间，先后有10余万人次购买了康东旭制作的健身课程。他坦言，运动健康是个1-100的事情，线上是通过教育的方式解决1-50的问题，余下51-100的问题都需要线下解决。</span></section><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1.259375\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"960\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/C4icBnA96NrWB5zEKXicpWkCKvRqoDayqb0HrbgwrkWpriaetc3pvtNbZmkGlMNBJaZsfxmdEXLRNKFaLtUCzQ4xA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1.8px;padding-right: 10px;padding-left: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">“线上用户基本上都是初级运动用户，动作的安全性是首要条件，所以在制作课程的时候需要很强的统筹能力和专业经验。”</span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">但是，康东旭也承认，线上的教练和直接交流的教练是有区别的，他解释说，“比如一个深蹲动作，如果线下教学，我看到会员的动作，就知道存在什么问题，然后我帮助会员解决。”</span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">“但线上课程，我看不到用户，因此我需要将深蹲练习会出现的所有问题都考虑进去，这对教练的专业性、经验积累就有了很高的要求。”</span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">康东旭希望有一天能帮助他们转化到线下完成剩下的提升，解决51-100的健康问题。他认为线上是培养健身者的积极性，而用户如果真的从线上进入线下，说明他们已经成为了重度健身爱好者，反而不会再从健身行业中流失了……</span></section><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;margin: 20px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;align-self: stretch;flex: 10 10 0%;background-color: rgb(255, 248, 246);height: auto;padding-top: 5px;padding-bottom: 5px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: center;font-size: 21px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.6;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">04</strong></p></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 80px;border-style: solid;border-width: 3px;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgb(255, 137, 89);flex: 0 0 auto;align-self: stretch;height: auto;margin-top: -15px;margin-right: -77px;margin-bottom: -15px;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section auto;background-color: rgb(255, 248, 246);flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: stretch;border-width: 0px;height: auto;padding: 5px 10px;border-top-style: solid;border-top-left-radius: 0px;border-top-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">官办健身房：实惠便民计划</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1.8px;padding-right: 10px;padding-left: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">2011年10月，上海市普陀区宜川百姓健身房正式投入运营，社区居民凭身份证、户口簿等即可办理健身卡。这是根据《上海市全民健身实施计划》的要求，申城将在“十二五”期间建成100家百姓健身房的第一家。</span></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-indent: 2em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">之后，杭州、温州、嘉兴也纷纷推出了百姓健身房。</span></section><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.5800781\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1024\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/C4icBnA96NrWB5zEKXicpWkCKvRqoDayqbzDb2640K4aTCcfBIBC0lCuCB7CX3BsL03QtgtKa1L8TjJhLqTbkw1g/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1.8px;padding-right: 10px;padding-left: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">     在温州，“百姓健身房”连续三年被列入温州市“十大民生实事”体育项目之一，并被评选为温州首届“微改革”最佳案例。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">     据温州市体育局公布的消息，截至2020年4月，全市已建成“百姓健身房”81家，注册会员3万余人，今年还计划新建165家百姓健身房。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">     疫情之下，百姓健身房的运营也受到了影响，不过管理部门已经迅速做出了调整。比如温州市体育局，就在官网上特别做出了通知，特别强调了会员卡延期的方案。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">     疫情给全球健身业带来了冲击，也带来了契机。就国内现行环境来说，疫情就像大浪淘沙，留下的是实力过硬的健身机构与从业者。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">     <strong>无论是线上还是线下，健身教练的专业度和服务意识，依旧是核心竞争力，也是提升会员黏度的关键因素。</strong></span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 46%;box-sizing: src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/C4icBnA96NrWB5zEKXicpWkCKvRqoDayqbFaULav2lP3RNVeRrIBPDKvdg42HiablSSic4U1usyjyvxfTBwYEBXMuw/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">是因为微信订阅号有了新的变动。公众号推送从以往按时间排序变成了智能排序了，也就是说你平时常看和常互动的订阅号更新会排在最前面。于是其他的推送就在推送消息里沉了底。</p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1.6740741\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/C4icBnA96NrWB5zEKXicpWkCKvRqoDayqbhIIlvwfvBMuYS85unKvc27y5icd88WReggmsmx0f17RFAZdRa3MicSBA/640?wx_fmt=png\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">变动带来的影响就是，假如你有几次没有点我们更新的推送，那么我们优秀的文章可能会逐渐被系统减少在你眼前出现的频率，直至消失在你的推送列表。那便是真正的告别了。</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 40%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.748\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"500\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/C4icBnA96NrWB5zEKXicpWkCKvRqoDayqbU7e8LI3iac0SBowgIjiaBibC5rAJPOu0ic3CGUyia3jsOebt3BdI8hYKvbg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">如果你不想错过如此优秀的文章，请多点进来看看。<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(98, 10, 10);box-sizing: border-box;\">并且在每次看完推送后，轻点一下文末的”在看“。点的次数越多，就能优先看到我们的深度好文。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(98, 10, 10);box-sizing: border-box;\">还有一个方法，就是把我们设为星标，这样就是我们新浪体育的忠实粉丝啦！</span></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"align-items: center;display: flex;margin-top: 15px;margin-bottom: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 1 0 1px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">是不是体育迷发现很久没有看到新浪体育的推文了，还以为新浪体育和微博热搜一样被整改了。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"align-items: center;display: flex;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 1 0 1px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 30px;height: 30px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 0 1 auto;padding-right: 5px;padding-left: 5px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-top: 20px;margin-right: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">当然不是！！</strong></p></section></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 1 0 1px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 30px;height: 30px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 80%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1.0756303\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"119\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/C4icBnA96NrWfnOlMjaaB6F7sDNjez9xEIN406kUrgTzDTrssTSn7p4CEibhHn4LZiapich2ZIibZvvR6pVLC0Xgtzw/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">是因为微信订阅号有了新的变动。公众号推送从以往按时间排序变成了智能排序了，也就是说你平时常看和常互动的订阅号更新会排在最前面。于是其他的推送就在推送消息里沉了底。</p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1.6740741\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/C4icBnA96NrWfnOlMjaaB6F7sDNjez9xEONHZ6wbuDEztbbkuWfXF5E8OLVy4FrzxThqeYmxQwZRuWib6Ue5QTmw/640?wx_fmt=png\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">变动带来的影响就是，假如你有几次没有点我们更新的推送，那么我们优秀的文章可能会逐渐被系统减少在你眼前出现的频率，直至消失在你的推送列表。那便是真正的告别了。</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 40%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.748\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"500\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/C4icBnA96NrWfnOlMjaaB6F7sDNjez9xEsnqibI0vsgvNqHwR05ojnz76hlpbHTBj278xB8f8FCjUcFibwwk0yvNg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">如果你不想错过如此优秀的文章，请多点进来看看。<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(98, 10, 10);box-sizing: border-box;\">并且在每次看完推送后，轻点一下文末的”在看“。点的次数越多，就能优先看到我们的深度好文。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(98, 10, 10);box-sizing: border-box;\">还有一个方法，就是把我们设为星标，这样就是我们新浪体育的忠实粉丝啦！</span></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"align-items: center;display:
